<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Vocabulary_List"> Vocabulary List </span></h2>
<p><i>A note about the IPA pronunciation guides here. The letters <b>/t/, /d/, /l/</b> and<b> /n/</b> are dental consonants which means that they are pronounced with the tongue touching the teeth which is different from how they are pronounced in English.</i>
</p><p><br />
</p>
<h3> <span class="mw-headline" id="A"> A </span></h3>
<ul><li><b>acchakat</b> [att͡ʃaˈkat] <span id="acchakat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to silence
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>acchak</b></small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Me vastoe hatif anni; ahhazaan yer nemo vacchaki.</b> &#8212; She will speak before me; until then you will keep yourself quiet.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>acchorkat</b> [att͡ʃoɾˈkat] <span id="acchorkat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to roll
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Che hash me vacchorka mae ki janeti majin me anokitta mae ki hrazefi.</b> &#8212; Or roll them in a rug and trample them with a horse.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>achra</b> [ˈat͡ʃɾa] <span id="achra"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> smelly
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>achrakh</b> [at͡ʃˈɾax] <span id="achrakh"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> smell
</dd><dd><i>ni.</i> stink
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>achralat</b> [at͡ʃɾaˈlat] <span id="achralat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to be smelly, to give off a smell
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>achra</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>adakhat</b> [adaˈxat] <span id="adakhat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to eat
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>adakh</b></small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Khaleesi zala meme adakha esinakh ajjalan.</b> &#8212; The khaleesi wants to eat something different tonight.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>adakhilat</b> [adaxiˈlat] <span id="adakhilat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to feed (specifically to feed on, or to feast on)
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>adakhi</b></small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Inte vadakhie tihoa.</b> &#8212; The beetles will feed on your eyes.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>addakhat</b> [addaˈxat] <span id="addakhat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to feed
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>addiwelat</b> [addiweˈlat] <span id="addiwelat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to moisten
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Shafka laz addiwee khirrof anni</b> &#8212; You can suck my dick.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>addo ajjalani</b> [ˈaddo ˈadd͡ʒalani] <span id="addo_ajjalani"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>np.</i> midnight
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>addothralat</b> [addoθɾaˈlat] <span id="addothralat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to convey, to transport someone
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>addothra</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>addrekat</b> [addɾeˈkat] <span id="addrekat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to cause to spill, to spill
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>addrivat</b> [addɾiˈvat] <span id="addrivat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to kill (chiefly when done intentionally by a person)
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>addriv</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ador</b> [aˈdor] <span id="ador"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> chair
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>adra</b> [ˈadɾa] <span id="adra"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>na.</i> turtle
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>aena</b> [ˈaena] <span id="aena"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>n.</i> morning
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>afazh</b> [aˈfaʒ] <span id="afazh"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> hot
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>afazhi</b> [ˈafaʒi] <span id="afazhi"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> warm
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>affa</b> [ˈaffa] <span id="affa"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>intj.</i> whoa! (horse command)
</dd><dd><i>intj.</i> "shh", sound used to calm a horse or a child
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>affazhat</b> [affaˈʒat] <span id="affazhat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to warm, to give warmth to, to make hot
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>affazolat</b> [affazoˈlat] <span id="affazolat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to replace
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>affazo</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>affesat</b> [affeˈsat] <span id="affesat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to make someone itch
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>affes</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>affin</b> [afˈfin] <span id="affin"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adv.</i> when
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Anha vazhak maan firikhnharen hoshora ma mahrazhi aqovi affin mori atihi mae.</b> &#8212; I will give to him a golden crown and men will tremble when they will see it.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>affisat</b> [affiˈsat] <span id="affisat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to clean, to wash
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>affis</b></small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Azhas maan affisat zis yeri, shekh ma shieraki anni.</b> &#8212; Let her clean your wound my sun and stars.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>afis</b> [aˈfis] <span id="afis"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>n.</i> fly
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>aggendat</b> [aggenˈdat] <span id="aggendat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to rip something, to tear something
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>aggend</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ahesh</b> [aˈheʃ] <span id="ahesh"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i> ni.</i> snow
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>aheshke</b> [aˈheʃke] <span id="aheshke"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i> ni.</i> winter
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>accusative: <b>aheshk</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ahhaqat</b> [ahhaˈqɑt] <span id="ahhaqat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to frustrate
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>ahhaqe</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ahhasat</b> [ahhaˈsat] <span id="ahhasat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to sharpen
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>ahhas</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ahhaz</b> [ahˈhaz] <span id="ahhaz"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adv.</i> then (of close or immediate future, compare to <b><a href="/Vocabulary#arrek" title="Vocabulary">arrek</a></b>)
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Me vastoe hatif anni; ahhazaan yer nemo vacchaki.</b> &#8212; She will speak before me; until then you will keep yourself quiet.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ai</b> [ˈai] <span id="ai"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>intj.</i> yes, obedient response
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ajjalan</b> [add͡ʒaˈlan] <span id="ajjalan"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adv.</i> tonight
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ajjin</b> [adˈd͡ʒin] <span id="ajjin"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adv.</i> now
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Jin chiorisi zafra ajjin, majin kisha ataki morea ven me vallayafa kisha.</b> &#8212; These women are slaves now to do with as we please.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akat</b> [aˈkat] <span id="akat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>num.</i> two
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akataki</b> [ˈakataki] <span id="akataki"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> second
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akka</b> [ˈakka] <span id="akka"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adv.</i> also, too, as well, even, even so, re-
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Rizhaan anni, vezh fin asaja rhaesheseres, maan anha valloshak azh akka.</b> &#8212; To my son, the stallion who will mount the world, I will also pledge a gift.</small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Anha soqe akka jin sacchey essheyi.</b> &#8212; I rewove this part of the top.</small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Kash athezar kishi vos akka.</b> &#8212; Not even when we leave.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akkate</b> [ˈakkate] <span id="akkate"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adv.</i> both, alike, the same way
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Zhavvorsa vadakhera ma hrazef ma vaf akkate.</b> &#8212; The dragon feeds on horse and lamb alike.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akkelenak</b> [akkeleˈnak] <span id="akkelenak"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>na.</i> leader
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akkelenat</b> [akkeleˈnat] <span id="akkelenat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to decide, to judge
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>Akko!</b> [ˈakko] <span id="akko"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>intj.</i> Stand up! (shortening of <b><a href="/Vocabulary#akkovarat" title="Vocabulary">akkovaras</a></b>; used to command animals)
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akkoalat</b> [akkoaˈlat] <span id="akkoalat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to heal
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>akkoal</b></small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Me akkoal hrazef k’athadavranazi ei mahrazhoa khalasari anni.</b> &#8212; He was better at healing horses than any man in my khalasar.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>akkovarat</b> [akkovaˈɾat] <span id="akkovarat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to stand (something) up
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>akkovar</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ale</b> [ˈale] <span id="ale"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> more
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Dalen rhaggat eveth ma ale vekhi she Vaes Seris.</b> &#8212; There are a thousand ships and more in the free cities.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>alegra</b> [aˈlegɾa] <span id="alegra"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> duck
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>accusative: <b>alegre</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>alikh</b> [aˈlix] <span id="alikh"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> more
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Kisha vastoki vos alikh hrazefi ido m'adori shiqethi.</b> &#8212; Let's speak no more about wooden horses or iron chairs.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>allayafat</b> [allajaˈfat] <span id="allayafat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to please
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>allayaf</b></small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Mori allayafi mae, jin alegra.</b> &#8212; She likes ducks.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>alle</b> [ˈalle] <span id="alle"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adv.</i> farther, further
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>alloshat</b> [alloˈʃat] <span id="alloshat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to pledge
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>allosh</b></small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Ma rizhaan anni, vezh fin asaja rhaesheseres, maan anha valloshak azh akka.</b> &#8212; And to my son, the stallion who will mount the world, I will also pledge a gift.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ammasat</b> [ammaˈsat] <span id="ammasat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to decorate
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>ammattelat</b> [ammatteˈlat] <span id="ammattelat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to hobble a person
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>ammatte</b></small></span>

<ul><li><b>ammemat</b> [ammeˈmat] <span id="ammemat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to play a musical instrument
</dd></dl>

</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>ammen</b></small></span>

</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to put an end to, to finish
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>annakho</b></small></span>

</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>annese</b> [ˈannese] <span id="annese"></span>
</li></ul>

</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zasqa</b> [ˈzasqɑ] <span id="zasqa"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> white
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zerqolat</b> [zerqɔˈlat] <span id="zerqolat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to swim
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhalia</b> [ˈʒalia] <span id="zhalia"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> butterfly
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>accusative: <b>zhalie</b></small></span>

<ul><li><b>zhani</b> [ˈʒani] <span id="zhani"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> spear
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>accusative: <b>zhan</b></small></span>

</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhav</b> [ʒav] <span id="zhav"></span>

<dl><dd><i>n.</i> lizard
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhavorsa</b> [ʒaˈvoɾsa] <span id="zhavorsa"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> dragon (<a href="/Vocabulary#zhavvorsa" title="Vocabulary">alternate pronunciation</a>)
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>accusative: <b>zhavors</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhavvorsa</b> [ʒavˈvoɾsa] <span id="zhavvorsa"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> dragon (<a href="/Vocabulary#zhavorsa" title="Vocabulary">alternate pronunciation</a>)
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>accusative: <b>zhavvors</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zheana</b> [ˈʒeana] <span id="zheana"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> beautiful (used for animate nouns)
</dd><dd><b>zheanalat</b> <i>vin.</i> to be beautiful (used for animate nouns)
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>zheana</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhey</b> [ʒej] <span id="zhey"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>part.</i> vocative particle
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Anha, zhey Drogo, atak jin.</b> &#8212; I, Drogo, will do this.</small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Zhey jalan atthirari anni. Hash azisi?</b> &#8212; Moon of my live. Are you hurt?</small></span>
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Hash yer ray tih loy alegra, zhey vikeesi?</b> &#8212; Have you seen any ducks, woman?</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhif</b> [ʒif] <span id="zhif"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>ni.</i> salt
</dd></dl>

</dd></dl>

<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> salty
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhikhat</b> [ʒiˈxat] <span id="zhikhat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>v.</i> to be sick
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>zhikh</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhilat</b> [ʒiˈlat] <span id="zhilat"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>vtr.</i> to love someone (used of romantic or sexual love; a private word)
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small>past SG: <b>zhil</b></small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhille</b> [ˈʒille] <span id="zhille"></span>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>det.</i> any
</dd><dd><span style="color:gray"><small><b>Okki zhille hrazef fin allayafa shafka drogikhoon anni.</b> &#8212; Choose any horse you wish from my herd.</small></span>
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>zhilli</b> [ˈʒilli] <span id="zhilli"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Abbreviations"> Abbreviations </span></h2>
<dl><dd><i>adj.</i> adjective
</dd><dd><i>adv.</i> adverb
</dd><dd><i>v. aux.</i> verbal auxiliary
</dd><dd><i>conj.</i> conjunction
</dd><dd><i>det.</i> determiner
</dd><dd><i>intj.</i> interjection
</dd><dd><i>n.</i> noun with unknown animacy
</dd><dd><i>na.</i> animate noun
</dd><dd><i>ni.</i> inanimate noun
</dd><dd><i>np.</i> noun phrase
</dd><dd><i>num.</i> numeral
</dd><dd><i>pn.</i> pronoun
</dd><dd><i>prep.</i> preposition
</dd><dd><i>prop. n.</i> proper noun
</dd><dd><i>v.</i> verb
</dd><dd><i>vin.</i> intransitive verb
</dd><dd><i>vtr.</i> transitive verb
</dd><dd><i>&#8594;nom.</i> assigns the following noun into nominative
</dd><dd><i>&#8594;acc.</i> assigns the following noun into accusative (not marked for verbs)
</dd><dd><i>&#8594;gen.</i> assigns the following noun into genitive
</dd><dd><i>&#8594;abl.</i> assigns the following noun into ablative
</dd><dd><i>&#8594;all.</i> assigns the following noun into allative
</dd></dl>

</p>
